## <a name="windows-server-2003-attributes"></a><span data-ttu-id="45e85-461">Atributos do Windows Server 2003</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="45e85-461">Windows Server 2003 Attributes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="45e85-462">Essa classe contém os seguintes atributos para o Windows Server 2003:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="45e85-462">This class contains the following attributes for Windows Server 2003:</span></span>

## <a name="windows-server-2003-r2-attributes"></a><span data-ttu-id="45e85-821">Atributos do Windows Server 2003 R2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="45e85-821">Windows Server 2003 R2 Attributes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="45e85-822">Essa classe contém os seguintes atributos para o Windows Server 2003 R2:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="45e85-822">This class contains the following attributes for Windows Server 2003 R2:</span></span>
